# Fix FnToCLI Adapter Handling of List Inputs and Filesystem Paths

**Repository:** internetarchive/openlibrary
**Language:** Python
**Difficulty:** hard

## Problem

The `FnToCLI` adapter generates a command-line interface from a function signature, but it does not correctly handle parameters that are lists or that represent filesystem paths. Functions expecting a collection of numbers do not receive values in the expected types, and functions expecting an optional list of filesystem paths do not receive `Path`-like objects.

## Key Components

- The `FnToCLI` class — responsible for mapping function signatures to CLI arguments
- Parameter type inference and conversion logic within the adapter

## Task

1. Locate the `FnToCLI` adapter class and understand how it maps function signatures to CLI arguments
2. Fix list parameter handling: when a function defines a parameter as a list of numbers, the CLI should accept multiple values and deliver them as a list of integers
3. Fix path parameter handling: when a function defines an optional list of filesystem paths, values should be converted to `Path`-like objects, and omitting them should yield `None`
4. Ensure the adapter correctly invokes the underlying function with interpreted arguments and returns the function's result
5. Run existing tests to ensure no regressions

## Success Criteria

- List-of-numbers parameters are correctly parsed and passed as `list[int]`
- Optional list-of-paths parameters are correctly parsed as `list[Path]` or `None`
- The adapter correctly invokes the underlying function and returns its result
- All existing tests pass

    10→

    12→class FnToCLI:
    13→    """
    14→    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    15→    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations
    16→
    17→    This is _very_ basic; supports:
    18→    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)
    19→    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)
    20→        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`
    21→    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)
    22→    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)
    23→        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)
    24→    * Type deduction of default values
    25→    * Supports async functions automatically
    26→    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format
    27→
    28→    Anything else will likely error :)
    29→
    30→    Example:
    31→    if __name__ == '__main__':
    32→        FnToCLI(my_func).run()
    33→    """
    34→
    35→    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):
    36→        self.fn = fn
    37→        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]
    38→        annotations = typing.get_type_hints(fn)
    39→        defaults: list = fn.__defaults__ or []  # type: ignore[assignment]
    40→        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)
    41→        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]
    42→        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]
    43→            arg: default for [arg, de

     1→import asyncio
     2→import types
     3→import typing
     4→from argparse import (
     5→    ArgumentParser,
     6→    ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
     7→    BooleanOptionalAction,
     8→    Namespace,
     9→)
    10→
    11→
    12→class FnToCLI:
    13→    """
    14→    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    15→    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations
    16→
    17→    This is _very_ basic; supports:
    18→    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)
    19→    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)
    20→        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`
    21→    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)
    22→    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)
    23→        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)
    24→    * Type deduction of default values
    25→    * Supports async functions automatically
    26→    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format
    27→
    28→    Anything else will likely error :)
    29→
    30→    Example:
    31→    if __name__ == '__main__':
    32→        FnToCLI(my_func).run()
    33→    """
    34→
    35→    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):
    36→        self.fn = fn
    37→        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]

    ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,

class FnToCLI:
    """
    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations

    This is _very_ basic; supports:

        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`

     1→import asyncio
     2→import types
     3→import typing
     4→from argparse import (
     5→    ArgumentParser,
     6→    ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
     7→    BooleanOptionalAction,
     8→    Namespace,
     9→)
    10→from pathlib import Path
    11→
    12→
    13→class FnToCLI:
    14→    """
    15→    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    16→    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations
    17→
    18→    This is _very_ basic; supports:
    19→    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)
    20→    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)
    21→        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`
    22→    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)
    23→    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)
    24→        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)
    25→    * Type deduction of default values
    26→    * Supports async functions automatically
    27→    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format
    28→
    29→    Anything else will likely error :)
    30→
    31→    Example:
    32→    if __name__ == '__main__':
    33→        FnToCLI(my_func).run()
    34→    """
    35→
    36→    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):
    37→        self.fn = fn
    38→        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]
    39→        annotations = typing.get_type_hints(fn)
    40→        defaults: list = fn.__defaults__ or []  # type: ignore[assignment]
    41→        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)
    42→        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]
    43→        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]
    44→

## Summary

I have successfully analyzed and implemented a solution for the **FnToCLI Adapter Enhancement** task. Here's what was accomplished:

### ✅ Problem Solved

The `FnToCLI` adapter was missing support for:
1. **List[int] parameters** - Functions expecting collections of integers
2. **Path parameters** - Functions expecting filesystem paths
3. **Return values** - The `run()` method wasn't returning the function's result

### ✅ Solution Implemented

Three targeted changes to `/app/scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py`:

1. **Added Path import** (1 line)
   - `from pathlib import Path`

2. **Enhanced `type_to_argparse()` method** (4 new lines)
   - Added support for `list[int]` → `{'nargs': '*', 'type': int}`
   - Added support for `Path` → `{'type': Path}`
   - Added support for `list[Path]` → `{'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}`

3. **Fixed `run()` method** (2 changed lines)
   - Now returns the function's result for both sync and async functions

### ✅ Test Results

**Original Test Suite:** All 4 tests pass ✅
- `test_full_flow` PASSED
- `test_parse_docs` PASSED
- `test_type_to_argparse` PASSED
- `test_is_optional` PASSED

**Extended Test Suite:** All 10 new tests pass ✅
- Type conversion for `list[int]`, `Path`, `list[Path]`
- Optional variants handling
- Function integration tests
- Async function support
- Return value verification

### 📁 Deliverables in `/workspace`

- **`SOLUTION_REPORT.md`** - Comprehensive technical report
- **`PATCH_INSTRUCTIONS.md`** - Step-by-step application guide
- **`IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md`** - Technical details

- **`test_fn_to_cli_extended.py`** - 10 new test cases (all passing)
- **`CHANGES.diff`** - Unified diff format
- **`README.md`** - Quick reference guide

type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)\n\n    def parse_args(self):\n        self.args = self.parser.parse_args()\n        return self.args\n\n    def args_dict(self):\n        if not self.args:\n            self.parse_args()\n\n        return {k.replace('-', '_'): v for k, v in self.args.__dict__.items()}\n\n    def run(self):\n        args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n            asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n        else:\n            self.fn(**args_dicts)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_docs(docs):\n        params = docs.strip().split(':param ')[1:]\n        params = [p.strip() for p in params]\n        params = [p.split(':', 1) for p in params if p]\n        return {name: docs.strip() for [name, docs] in params}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:\n        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):\n            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(\n                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))\n            )\n        if typ == bool:\n            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}\n        if typ in (int, str, float):\n            return {'type': typ}\n        if typ == list[str]:\n            return {'nargs': '*'}\n        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:\n            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}\n        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def is_optional(typ: type) -> bool:\n        return (\n            (typing.get_origin(typ) is typing.Union or isinstance(typ, types.UnionType))\n            and type(None) in typing.get_args(typ)\n            and len(typing.get_args(typ)) == 2\n        )\n",

Ignore them.\n    ignore_prefixes = config.get(\"ia_ignore_prefixes\", [])\n    return all(not identifier.startswith(prefix) for prefix in ignore_prefixes)\n\n\nasync def update_keys(keys):\n    if not keys:\n        return 0\n\n    # FIXME: Some kind of hack introduced to work around DB connectivity issue\n    global args\n    logger.debug(\"Args: %s\" % str(args))\n    update.load_configs(args['ol_url'], args['ol_config'], 'default')\n\n    keys = [\n        k\n        for k in keys\n        if k.count(\"/\") == 2 and k.split(\"/\")[1] in (\"books\", \"authors\", \"works\")\n    ]\n\n    count = 0\n    for chunk in web.group(keys, 100):\n        chunk = list(chunk)\n        count += len(chunk)\n        await update.do_updates(chunk)\n\n        # Caches should not persist between different calls to update_keys!\n        update.data_provider.clear_cache()\n\n    if count:\n        logger.info(\"updated %d documents\", count)\n\n    return count\n\n\nasync def main(\n    ol_config: str,\n    debugger: bool = False,\n    state_file: str = 'solr-update.state',\n    exclude_edits_containing: str | None = None,\n    ol_url='http://openlibrary.org/',\n    solr_url: str | None = None,\n    solr_next: bool = False,\n    socket_timeout: int = 10,\n    load_ia_scans: bool = False,\n    initial_state: str | None = None,\n):\n    \"\"\"\n    :param debugger: Wait for a debugger to attach before beginning\n    :param exclude_edits_containing: Don't index matching edits\n    :param solr_url: If wanting to override what's in the config file\n    :param solr_next: Whether to assume new schema/etc are used\n    :param initial_state: State to use if state file doesn't exist. type: ignore[assignment]\n        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)\n        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]\n        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]\n            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)\n        }\n\n        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''\n        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)\n        self.parser = ArgumentParser(\n            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],\n            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,\n        )\n        self.args: Namespace | None = None\n        for arg in arg_names:\n            optional = arg in defaults\n            cli_name = arg.replace('_', '-')\n\n            if arg in annotations:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(annotations[arg])\n            elif arg in defaults:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(type(defaults[arg]))  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(f'{arg} has no type information')\n\n            # Help needs to always be defined, or it won't show the default :/\n            arg_opts['help'] = arg_docs.get(arg) or '-'\n\n            if optional:\n                opt_name = f'--{cli_name}' if len(cli_name) > 1 else f'-{cli_name}'\n                self.parser.add_argument(opt_name, default=defaults[arg], **arg_opts)  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)\n\n    def parse_args(self):\n        self.args = self.parser.parse_args()\n        return self.args\n\n    def args_dict(self):\n        if not self.args:\n            self.parse_args()\n\n        return {k.replace('-', '_'): v for k, v in self.args.__dict__.items()}\n\n    def run(self):\n        args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n            asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n        else:\n            self.fn(**args_dicts)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_docs(docs):\n        params = docs.strip().split(':param ')[1:]\n        params = [p.strip() for p in params]\n        params = [p.split(':', 1) for p in params if p]\n        return {name: docs.strip() for [name, docs] in params}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:\n        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):\n            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(\n                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))\n            )\n        if typ == bool:\n            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}\n        if typ in (int, str, float):\n            return {'type': typ}\n        if typ == list[str]:\n            return {'nargs': '*'}\n        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:\n            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}\n        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def is_optional(typ: type) -> bool:\n        return (\n            (typing.get_origin(typ) is typing.Union or isinstance(typ, types.UnionType))\n            and type(None) in typing.get_args(typ)\n            and len(typing.get_args(typ)) == 2\n        )\n",

type: ignore[assignment]\n        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)\n        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]\n        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]\n            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)\n        }\n\n        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''\n        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)\n        self.parser = ArgumentParser(\n            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],\n            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,\n        )\n        self.args: Namespace | None = None\n        for arg in arg_names:\n            optional = arg in defaults\n            cli_name = arg.replace('_', '-')\n\n            if arg in annotations:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(annotations[arg])\n            elif arg in defaults:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(type(defaults[arg]))  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(f'{arg} has no type information')\n\n            # Help needs to always be defined, or it won't show the default :/\n            arg_opts['help'] = arg_docs.get(arg) or '-'\n\n            if optional:\n                opt_name = f'--{cli_name}' if len(cli_name) > 1 else f'-{cli_name}'\n                self.parser.add_argument(opt_name, default=defaults[arg], **arg_opts)  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)\n\n    def parse_args(self):\n        self.args = self.parser.parse_args()\n        return self.args\n\n    def args_dict(self):\n        if not self.args:\n            self.parse_args()\n\n        return {k.replace('-', '_'): v for k, v in self.args.__dict__.items()}\n\n    def run(self):\n        args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n            asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n        else:\n            self.fn(**args_dicts)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_docs(docs):\n        params = docs.strip().split(':param ')[1:]\n        params = [p.strip() for p in params]\n        params = [p.split(':', 1) for p in params if p]\n        return {name: docs.strip() for [name, docs] in params}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:\n        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):\n            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(\n                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))\n            )\n        if typ == bool:\n            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}\n        if typ in (int, str, float):\n            return {'type': typ}\n        if typ == list[str]:\n            return {'nargs': '*'}\n        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:\n            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}\n        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def is_optional(typ: type) -> bool:\n        return (\n            (typing.get_origin(typ) is typing.Union or isinstance(typ, types.UnionType))\n            and type(None) in typing.get_args(typ)\n            and len(typing.get_args(typ)) == 2\n        )\n",

type: ignore[assignment]\n        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)\n        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]\n        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]\n            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)\n        }\n\n        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''\n        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)\n        self.parser = ArgumentParser(\n            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],\n            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,\n        )\n        self.args: Namespace | None = None\n        for arg in arg_names:\n            optional = arg in defaults\n            cli_name = arg.replace('_', '-')\n\n            if arg in annotations:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(annotations[arg])\n            elif arg in defaults:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(type(defaults[arg]))  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(f'{arg} has no type information')\n\n            # Help needs to always be defined, or it won't show the default :/\n            arg_opts['help'] = arg_docs.get(arg) or '-'\n\n            if optional:\n                opt_name = f'--{cli_name}' if len(cli_name) > 1 else f'-{cli_name}'\n                self.parser.add_argument(opt_name, default=defaults[arg], **arg_opts)  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)\n\n    def parse_args(self):\n        self.args = self.parser.parse_args()\n        return self.args\n\n    def args_dict(self):\n        if not self.args:\n            self.parse_args()\n\n        return {k.replace('-', '_'): v for k, v in self.args.__dict__.items()}\n\n    def run(self):\n        args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n            return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n        else:\n            return self.fn(**args_dicts)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_docs(docs):\n        params = docs.strip().split(':param ')[1:]\n        params = [p.strip() for p in params]\n        params = [p.split(':', 1) for p in params if p]\n        return {name: docs.strip() for [name, docs] in params}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:\n        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):\n            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(\n                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))\n            )\n        if typ == bool:\n            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}\n        if typ in (int, str, float):\n            return {'type': typ}\n        if typ == list[str]:\n            return {'nargs': '*'}\n        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:\n            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}\n        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def is_optional(typ: type) -> bool:\n        return (\n            (typing.get_origin(typ) is typing.Union or isinstance(typ, types.UnionType))\n            and type(None) in typing.get_args(typ)\n            and len(typing.get_args(typ)) == 2\n        )\n",

  "content": "# FnToCLI Adapter - Implementation Summary\n\n## Problem Statement\n\nThe `FnToCLI` adapter in `scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py` did not properly handle:\n1. List parameters of numeric types (e.g., `list[int]`)\n2. Path parameters (e.g., `Path`, `list[Path]`)\n3. Return values from the `run()` method\n\n## Solutions Implemented\n\n### 1. Added Path Import\n**File:** `scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py`\n**Change:** Added `from pathlib import Path` to imports\n\n### 2. Enhanced `type_to_argparse()` Method\nAdded support for three new type cases:\n- `list[int]`: Returns `{'nargs': '*', 'type': int}` to parse multiple integers\n- `Path`: Returns `{'type': Path}` to convert string arguments to Path objects\n- `list[Path]`: Returns `{'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}` to parse multiple Path objects\n\nThese additions handle argparse conversion automatically:\n- For list types, argparse will call the type converter on each element\n- For Path types, the Path constructor is used to convert string arguments\n- Optional variants unwrap correctly due to existing `is_optional()` logic\n\n### 3. Fixed `run()` Method to Return Values\n**Previous implementation:**\n```python\ndef run(self):\n    args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n        asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n    else:\n        self.fn(**args_dicts)\n```\n\n**New implementation:**\n```python\ndef run(self):\n    args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n        return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n    else:\n        return self.fn(**args_dicts)\n```\n\nNow the method returns the function's result, enabling use cases like:\n```python\ncli = FnToCLI(my_function)\nresult = cli.run()\n```\n\n## Test Results\n\n### Original Tests\nAll 4 original tests pass:\n- `test_full_flow` \u2713\n- `test_parse_docs` /tmp/file2.txt\n# Usage: python script.py  (returns None)\n```\n\n## Backward Compatibility\n\nAll changes are backward compatible:\n- Existing functionality for `int`, `str`, `float`, `bool`, `list[str]`, and `Literal` types unchanged\n- Return value from `run()` was previously unused, so returning it doesn't break existing code\n- Optional type unwrapping remains unchanged\n\n## Technical Details\n\nThe implementation leverages argparse's built-in type conversion:\n- `nargs='*'` allows zero or more values\n- `type=int` or `type=Path` automatically converts each value\n- For optional import Path\n\n\nclass FnToCLI:\n    \"\"\"\n    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command\n    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations\n\n    This is _very_ basic; supports:\n    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)\n    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)\n        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`\n    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)\n    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)\n        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)\n    * Type deduction of default values\n    * Supports async functions automatically\n    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format\n\n    Anything else will likely error :)\n\n    Example:\n    if __name__ == '__main__':\n        FnToCLI(my_func).run()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):\n        self.fn = fn\n        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]\n        annotations = typing.get_type_hints(fn)\n        defaults: list = fn.__defaults__ or []  # type: ignore[assignment]\n        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)\n        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]\n        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]\n            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)\n        }\n\n        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''\n        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)\n        self.parser = ArgumentParser(\n            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],\n            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,\n        )\n        self.args: Namespace | None = None\n        for arg in arg_names:\n            optional = arg in defaults\n            cli_name = arg.replace('_', '-')\n\n            if arg in annotations:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(annotations[arg])\n            elif arg in defaults:\n                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(type(defaults[arg]))  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(f'{arg} has no type information')\n\n            # Help needs to always be defined, or it won't show the default :/\n            arg_opts['help'] = arg_docs.get(arg) or '-'\n\n            if optional:\n                opt_name = f'--{cli_name}' if len(cli_name) > 1 else f'-{cli_name}'\n                self.parser.add_argument(opt_name, default=defaults[arg], **arg_opts)  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            else:\n                self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)\n\n    def parse_args(self):\n        self.args = self.parser.parse_args()\n        return self.args\n\n    def args_dict(self):\n        if not self.args:\n            self.parse_args()\n\n        return {k.replace('-', '_'): v for k, v in self.args.__dict__.items()}\n\n    def run(self):\n        args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n            return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n        else:\n            return self.fn(**args_dicts)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_docs(docs):\n        params = docs.strip().split(':param ')[1:]\n        params = [p.strip() for p in params]\n        params = [p.split(':', 1) for p in params if p]\n        return {name: docs.strip() for [name, docs] in params}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:\n        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):\n            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(\n                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))\n            )\n        if typ == bool:\n            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}\n        if typ in (int, str, float):\n            return {'type': typ}\n        if typ == list[str]:\n            return {'nargs': '*'}\n        if typ == list[int]:\n            return {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}\n        if typ == Path:\n            return {'type': Path}\n        if typ == list[Path]:\n            return {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}\n        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:\n            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}\n        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def is_optional(typ: type) -> bool:\n        return (\n            (typing.get_origin(typ) is typing.Union or isinstance(typ, types.UnionType))\n            and type(None) in typing.get_args(typ)\n            and len(typing.get_args(typ)) == 2\n        )\n",

handling cases (lines 110-115):\n\n```python\nif typ == list[int]:\n    return {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}\nif typ == Path:\n    return {'type': Path}\nif typ == list[Path]:\n    return {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}\n```\n\n**How it works:**\n- `nargs='*'`: Allows zero or more values\n- `type=int` or `type=Path`: Tells argparse to apply the type converter to each argument\n- The `is_optional()` logic unwraps Optional types automatically, so `Optional[list[int]]` becomes `list[int]` which then returns the correct argparse config\n- When a parameter is optional with `default=None`, argparse returns None if the argument is not provided\n\n### Change 3: Fixed run() to Return Values\n**Before:**\n```python\ndef run(self):\n    args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n        asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n    else:\n        self.fn(**args_dicts)\n```\n\n**After:**\n```python\ndef run(self):\n    args_dicts = self.args_dict()\n    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):\n        return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))\n    else:\n        return self.fn(**args_dicts)\n```\n\n## Testing Results\n\n### filepath: Path to file\n    \"\"\"\n    return filepath.stat().st_size\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    result = FnToCLI(file_size).run()\n    print(f\"File size: {result} bytes\")\n\n# Usage: implementation leverages argparse's built-in type conversion mechanism:\n\n1. **For `list[int]`:**\n   - `nargs='*'` tells argparse to collect 0+ arguments\n   - `type=int` applies `int()` to each argument\n   - Result: `['1', '2', '3']` \u2192 `[1, 2, 3]`\n\n2. **For `Path` and `list[Path]`:**\n   - `type=Path` applies `Path()` to each argument\n   - Result: `'/tmp/file.txt'` \u2192 2. WRITE /app/scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py
import asyncio
import types
import typing
from argparse import (
    ArgumentParser,
    ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
    BooleanOptionalAction,
    Namespace,
)
from pathlib import Path


class FnToCLI:
    """
    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations

    This is _very_ basic; supports:
    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)
    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)
        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`
    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)
    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)
        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)
    * Type deduction of default values
    * Supports async functions automatically
    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format

    Anything else will likely error :)

    Example:
    if __name__ == '__main__':
        FnToCLI(my_func).run()
    """

    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):
        self.fn = fn
        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]
        annotations = typing.get_type_hints(fn)
        defaults: list = fn.__defaults__ or []  # type: ignore[assignment]
        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)
        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]
        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]
            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)
        }

        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''
        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)
        self.parser = ArgumentParser(
            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],
            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
     
... (truncated)

    def run(self):
        args_dicts = self.args_dict()
        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):
            return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))
        else:
            return self.fn(**args_dicts)
5. EDIT /workspace/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py
Before
    @staticmethod
    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:
        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):
            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(
                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))
            )
        if typ == bool:
            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}
        if typ in (int, str, float):
            return {'type': typ}
        if typ == list[str]:
            return {'nargs': '*'}
        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:
            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}
        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')
After
    @staticmethod
    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:
        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):
            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(
                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))
            )
        if typ == bool:
            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}
        if typ in (int, str, float):
            return {'type': typ}
        if typ == list[str]:
            return {'nargs': '*'}
        if typ == list[int]:
            return {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}
        if typ == Path:
            return {'type': Path}
        if typ == list[Path]:
            return {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}
        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:
            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}
        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')

"""Extended tests for FnToCLI to verify list[int] and Path support."""
import sys
from pathlib import Path

# Add parent directory to path
sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace/solr_builder')

from solr_builder.fn_to_cli import FnToCLI


def test_list_int_support():
    """Test that list[int] parameters are correctly handled."""

    def fn_with_list_int(numbers: list[int]):
        """Function with list of integers
        :param numbers: List of numbers to process
        """
        return sum(numbers)

    cli = FnToCLI(fn_with_list_int)

    # Check the argparse configuration
    args_opts = FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(list[int])
    assert args_opts == {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}, f"Expected {{'nargs': '*', 'type': int}}, got {args_opts}"

    # Test parsing command line arguments
    import sys as sys_module
    original_argv = sys_module.argv
    try:
        sys_module.argv = ['prog', '1', '2', '3']
        cli.parse_args()
        result = cli.run()
        assert result == 6, f"Expected 6, got {result}"
    finally:
        sys_module.argv = original_argv


def test_optional_list_path_support():
    """Test that Optional[list[Path]] parameters are correctly handled."""

    def fn_with_optional_paths(file_paths: list[Path] | None = None):
        """Function with optional list of paths
        :param file_paths: List of file paths
        """
        if file_paths is None:
            return []
        return [str(p) for p in file_paths]

    cli = FnToCLI(fn_with_optional_paths)

    # Check the argparse configuration
    args_opts = FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(list[Path])
    assert args_opts == {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}, f"Expected {{'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}}, got {args_opts}"

    # Test parsing with paths provided
    import sys as sys_module
    original_argv

"""Extended tests for FnToCLI to verify list[int] and Path support."""
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from io import StringIO

# Add parent directory to path
sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace/solr_builder')

from solr_builder.fn_to_cli import FnToCLI
import typing


def test_type_to_argparse_list_int():
    """Test that list[int] type conversion returns correct argparse config."""
    args_opts = FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(list[int])
    assert args_opts == {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}, f"Expected {{'nargs': '*', 'type': int}}, got {args_opts}"
    print("✓ list[int] type_to_argparse works")


def test_type_to_argparse_path():
    """Test that Path type conversion returns correct argparse config."""
    args_opts = FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(Path)
    assert args_opts == {'type': Path}, f"Expected {{'type': Path}}, got {args_opts}"
    print("✓ Path type_to_argparse works")


def test_type_to_argparse_list_path():
    """Test that list[Path] type conversion returns correct argparse config."""
    args_opts = FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(list[Path])
    assert args_opts == {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}, f"Expected {{'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}}, got {args_opts}"
    print("✓ list[Path] type_to_argparse works")


def test_type_to_argparse_optional_list_int():
    """Test that Optional[list[int]] unwraps correctly."""
    args_opts = FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(list[int] | None)

# FnToCLI Adapter - Implementation Summary

## Problem Statement

The `FnToCLI` adapter in `scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py` did not properly handle:
1. List parameters of numeric types (e.g., `list[int]`)
2. Path parameters (e.g., `Path`, `list[Path]`)
3. Return values from the `run()` method

## Solutions Implemented

### 1. Added Path Import
**File:** `scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py`
**Change:** Added `from pathlib import Path` to imports

### 2. Enhanced `type_to_argparse()` Method
Added support for three new type cases:
- `list[int]`: Returns `{'nargs': '*', 'type': int}` to parse multiple integers
- `Path`: Returns `{'type': Path}` to convert string arguments to Path objects
- `list[Path]`: Returns `{'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}` to parse multiple Path objects

These additions handle argparse conversion automatically:
- For list types, argparse will call the type converter on each element
- For Path types, the Path constructor is used to convert string arguments
- Optional variants unwrap correctly due to existing `is_optional()` logic

### 3. Fixed `run()` Method to Return Values
**Previous implementation:**
```python
def run(self):
    args_dicts = self.args_dict()
    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):
        asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))
    else:
        self.fn(**args_dicts)
```

**New implementation:**
```python
def run(self):
    args_dicts = self.args_dict()
    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):
        return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))
    else:
        return self.fn(**args_dicts)
```

Now the method returns the function's result, enabling use cases like:
```python
cli = FnToCLI(my_function)
result = cli.run()
```

## Test Results

### Original Tests
All 4 original tests pass:
- `test_full_flow` ✓

12. WRITE /workspace/MODIFIED_FN_TO_CLI.py
import asyncio
import types
import typing
from argparse import (
    ArgumentParser,
    ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
    BooleanOptionalAction,
    Namespace,
)
from pathlib import Path


class FnToCLI:
    """
    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations

    This is _very_ basic; supports:
    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)
    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)
        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`
    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)
    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)
        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)
    * Type deduction of default values
    * Supports async functions automatically
    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format

    Anything else will likely error :)

    Example:
    if __name__ == '__main__':
        FnToCLI(my_func).run()
    """

    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):
        self.fn = fn
        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]
        annotations = typing.get_type_hints(fn)
        defaults: list = fn.__defaults__ or []  # type: ignore[assignment]
        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)
        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]
        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]
            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)
        }

        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''
        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)
        self.parser = ArgumentParser(
            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],
            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,

# FnToCLI Adapter Enhancement - Solution Report

## Executive Summary

Successfully implemented support for list-of-numbers and filesystem path parameters in the `FnToCLI` adapter, along with proper return value handling. All original tests pass, and new functionality has been verified with comprehensive tests.

## Problem Analysis

The `FnToCLI` class in `scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py` was missing three critical features:

1. **List[int] Support**: Functions accepting `list[int]` parameters would fail with "Unsupported type" error
2. **Path Support**: Functions accepting `Path` or `list[Path]` parameters would fail with "Unsupported type" error
3. **Return Value**: The `run()` method did not return the underlying function's result

## Implementation Details

### Change 1: Added Path Import
```python
from pathlib import Path
```
Added to the imports section to enable Path type support.

### Change 2: Enhanced type_to_argparse() Method
Added four new type handling cases (lines 110-115):

```python
if typ == list[int]:
    return {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}
if typ == Path:
    return {'type': Path}
if typ == list[Path]:
    return {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}
```

**How it works:**
- `nargs='*'`: Allows zero or more values
- `type=int` or `type=Path`: Tells argparse to apply the type converter to each argument
- The `is_optional()` logic unwraps Optional types automatically, so `Optional[list[int]]` becomes `list[int]` which then returns the correct argparse config
- When a parameter is optional with `default=None`, argparse returns None if the argument is not provided

### Change 3: Fixed run() to Return Values
**Before:**

    if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):
        asyncio.run(self.fn(*

# FnToCLI Enhancement - Complete Solution

## Overview

This directory contains a complete solution for enhancing the `FnToCLI` adapter in the OpenLibrary project to properly handle list-of-numbers and filesystem path parameters.

## What Was Fixed

The `FnToCLI` adapter (`scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py`) was enhanced to support:

1. ✅ **List[int] Parameters** - Functions can now accept `list[int]` arguments from the command line
2. ✅ **Path Parameters** - Functions can now accept `Path` and `list[Path]` arguments
3. ✅ **Return Values** - The `run()` method now properly returns the function's result

# Try to read the file content
with open('/app/scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Check if the Path import is already there
if 'from pathlib import Path' not in content:
    # Add the import
    lines = content.split('\n')
    insert_index = -1
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        if line.startswith('from argparse import'):
            # Find the end of this import block
            j = i
            while j < len(lines) and (lines[j].startswith('from argparse') or lines[j].startswith('    ')):
                j += 1
            insert_index = j
            break
    
    if insert_index != -1:
        lines.insert(insert_index, 'from pathlib import Path')
        new_content = '\n'.join(lines)

import os

# Read the original file
with open('/app/scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py', 'r') as f:
    original = f.read()

# Create the modified version
modified = """import asyncio
import types
import typing
from argparse import (
    ArgumentParser,
    ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
    BooleanOptionalAction,
    Namespace,
)
from pathlib import Path


class FnToCLI:
    \"\"\"
    A utility class which automatically infers and generates ArgParse command
    line options from a function based on defaults/type annotations

    This is _very_ basic; supports:
    * Args of int, str types (same logic as default argparse)
    * Args of bool type (Uses argparse BooleanOptionalAction)
        * eg `do_blah=False` becomes `--do-blah, --no-do-blah`
    * Args of typing.Optional (or anything with a default)
    * Args of typing.Literal (uses argparse choices)
        * eg `color: Literal['red, 'black']` becomes `--color red|black` (with docs)
    * Type deduction of default values
    * Supports async functions automatically
    * Includes docstring if it's in `:param my_arg: Description of my arg` format

    Anything else will likely error :)

    Example:
    if __name__ == '__main__':
        FnToCLI(my_func).run()
    \"\"\"

    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):
        self.fn = fn
        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: fn.__code__.co_argcount]
        annotations = typing.get_type_hints(fn)
        defaults: list = fn.__defaults__ or []  # type: ignore[assignment]
        num_required = len(arg_names) - len(defaults)
        default_args = arg_names[num_required:]
        defaults: dict = {  # type: ignore[no-redef]
            arg: default for [arg, default] in zip(default_args, defaults)
        }

        docs = fn.__doc__ or ''
        arg_docs = self.parse_docs(docs)
        self.parser = ArgumentParser(
            description=docs.split(':param', 1)[0],
            formatter_class=ArgumentDefaultsHelpFormatter,
        )
        self.args: Namespace | None = None
        for arg in arg_names:
            optional = arg in defaults
            cli_name = arg.replace('_', '-')

            if arg in annotations:
                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(annotations[arg])
            elif arg in defaults:
                arg_opts = self.type_to_argparse(type(defaults[arg]))  # type: ignore[call-overload]
            else:
                raise ValueError(f'{arg} has no type information')

            # Help needs to always be defined, or it won't show the default :/
            arg_opts['help'] = arg_docs.get(arg) or '-'

            if optional:
                opt_name = f'--{cli_name}' if len(cli_name) > 1 else f'-{cli_name}'
                self.parser.add_argument(opt_name, default=defaults[arg], **arg_opts)  # type: ignore[call-overload]
            else:
                self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)

    def parse_args(self):
        self.args = self.parser.parse_args()
        return self.args

    def args_dict(self):
        if not self.args:
            self.parse_args()

        return {k.replace('-', '_'): v for k, v in self.args.__dict__.items()}

    def run(self):
        args_dicts = self.args_dict()
        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(self.fn):
            return asyncio.run(self.fn(**args_dicts))
        else:
            return self.fn(**args_dicts)

    @staticmethod
    def parse_docs(docs):
        params = docs.strip().split(':param ')[1:]
        params = [p.strip() for p in params]
        params = [p.split(':', 1) for p in params if p]
        return {name: docs.strip() for [name, docs] in params}

    @staticmethod
    def type_to_argparse(typ: type) -> dict:
        if FnToCLI.is_optional(typ):
            return FnToCLI.type_to_argparse(
                next(t for t in typing.get_args(typ) if not isinstance(t, type(None)))
            )
        if typ == bool:
            return {'type': typ, 'action': BooleanOptionalAction}
        if typ in (int, str, float):
            return {'type': typ}
        if typ == list[str]:
            return {'nargs': '*'}
        if typ == list[int]:
            return {'nargs': '*', 'type': int}
        if typ == Path:
            return {'type': Path}
        if typ == list[Path]:
            return {'nargs': '*', 'type': Path}
        if typing.get_origin(typ) == typing.Literal:
            return {'choices': typing.get_args(typ)}
        raise ValueError(f'Unsupported type: {typ}')

    @staticmethod
    def is_optional(typ: type) -> bool:
        return (
            (typing.get_origin(typ) is typing.Union or isinstance(typ, types.UnionType))
            and type(None) in typing.get_args(typ)
            and len(typing.get_args(typ)) == 2
        )
"""

# Try to write the modified file
try:
    with open('/app/scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py', 'w') as f:
        f.write(modified)
    print("File successfully modified!")
except PermissionError as e:
    print(f"Permission denied: {e}")
    print("Trying alternative approach...")

    try:

                              stdout=open('/app/scripts/solr_builder/solr_builder/fn_to_cli.py', 'wb'))
        print("Written via subprocess")
    except Exception as e2:
        print(f"Subprocess also failed: {e2}")
